```sql
-- drop tableif exists #diffCFD

SELECT 'Gap' AS Category
	 , 'Gap_CFD' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , sum(a.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(a.USDValue  ) as USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,a.IsDLTUser
-- into #diffCFD
FROM 
(
-------------**** calculated close ******* ------------------

SELECT * from (
	SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
	 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_CFD' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #calculatedBalanceCFD
from 
(
		
		SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
			 , 'OpeningBalanceCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
			 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #openingbalanceCFD
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]>
		AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%CFD%'
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'BuyCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)

			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD

		AND bdidb.Metric = 'BuyCFD'

			 ,IsDLTUser

		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'FullCommissionCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming

			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition

		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD4
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'SellCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits,
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD4
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'SellCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		) a
GROUP BY 
a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser) obc
UNION ALL 
	SELECT obc.Category
			   , obc.Metric
			   , obc.PositionType
			   , obc.Name
			   , obc.PositionTiming
			   , -1 * obc.TotalUnits AS TotalUnits
			   , -1 * obc.USDValue AS USDValue
			   , obc.IsValidCustomer
			   , obc.IsCreditReportValidCB
			   , obc.IsOutlier
			   , obc.OutlierTransition
			   , obc.CFD_Real_Filter 
			   ,IsDLTUser
----- ********  closing balance again ******** -----
			FROM 
	(
			SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
	 , 'ClosingBalanceCFD' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #closingbalanceCFD
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%CFD%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceCFD'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,IsDLTUser
			) obc
) a
GROUP BY 
	   a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all 


-- drop table if exists #OpeningBalance

SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
	 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #OpeningBalance
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
		bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all

	 , 'ClosingBalanceReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #ClosingBalance

WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceReal'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name

	   bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming

-- drop table if exists #txReal

Select 'TX' AS Category
	 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		AS USDValue
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #txReal
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all

	 , - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		AS TotalUnits
	 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
	 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		AS USDValue
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser

---- ****** calculated balance ********------

-- drop table if exists #calculatedBalance

SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
	 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_Real' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #calculatedBalance
		from 
		(
			SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
			 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
			 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #OpeningBalance
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]>
		AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
				bdidb.Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal1
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'ValidZeroReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal1
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'ValidZeroReal')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal2
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'InValidZeroReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal2
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'InValidZeroReal')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all

				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)

			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			 , - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
			 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue

			,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				, - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue

			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB

			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter

			 , bdidb.Name

			 , 'RedeemStakingSell' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType

			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				,- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)

		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemStakingSell')

		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,IsDLTUser
		) a
GROUP BY 
a.Category
	 , a. Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser


UNION ALL 

---- ******* gap ******** ------

-- drop table if exists #diffReal 

SELECT 'Gap' AS Category
	 , 'Gap_Real' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , sum(a.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(a.USDValue  ) as USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #diffReal
FROM 
(
SELECT * from (
				SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
						 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_Real' AS Metric
						 , a.PositionType
						 , a.Name
						 , a.PositionTiming
						 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
						 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
						 , a.IsValidCustomer
						 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
						 , a.IsOutlier
						 , a.OutlierTransition
						 , a.Real_Real_Filter
						 ,IsDLTUser
					-- into #calculatedBalance
							from 
							(
								SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
								 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
								 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #OpeningBalance
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]>
							AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
							AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
									bdidb.Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal1
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'ValidZeroReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal1
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'ValidZeroReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal2
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'InValidZeroReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal2
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'InValidZeroReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal3
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'FullCommissionReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal3
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'FullCommissionReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name

								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal4
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'TX_Real' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)

								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal4

							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'StakingBuy')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name

							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'RedeemBuy' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType

								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)

								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal5

								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal6
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'RedeemStakingBuy' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal6
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemStakingBuy')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal7
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'SellReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
								 , - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
								 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal7
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'SellReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal8
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'RedeemSell' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
								,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									, - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal8
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemSell')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal9
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'StakingSell' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
								,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									,- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal9
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'StakingSell')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal10
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'RedeemStakingSell' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
								,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									,- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal10
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 1]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemStakingSell')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,IsDLTUser
							) a
					GROUP BY 
					a.Category
						 , a. Metric
						 , a.PositionType
						 , a.Name
						 , a.PositionTiming
						 , a.IsValidCustomer
						 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
						 , a.IsOutlier
						 , a.OutlierTransition
						 , a.Real_Real_Filter
						 ,IsDLTUser

				) obc
UNION ALL SELECT obc.Category
			   , obc.Metric
			   , obc.PositionType
			   , obc.Name
			   , obc.PositionTiming
			   , -1 * obc.TotalUnits AS TotalUnits
			   , -1 * obc.USDValue AS USDValue
			   , obc.IsValidCustomer
			   , obc.IsCreditReportValidCB
			   , obc.IsOutlier
			   , obc.OutlierTransition
			   , obc.Real_Real_Filter 
			   ,IsDLTUser
							FROM (
								SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
					 , 'ClosingBalanceReal' AS Metric
					 , bdidb.PositionType
					 , bdidb.Name
					 , bdidb.PositionTiming
					 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
					 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
					 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
					 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
					 , bdidb.IsOutlier
					 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
					 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
					 ,IsDLTUser
					-- into #ClosingBalance
					FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
					WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 2]>
					AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
					AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceReal'
					-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
					GROUP BY 
					   bdidb.Metric
					 , bdidb.PositionType
					 , bdidb.Name
					 , bdidb.PositionTiming
					 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
					 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
					 , bdidb.IsOutlier
					 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
					 ,IsDLTUser
				) obc
) a
GROUP BY 
	   a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,IsDLTUser
```

### 15. Custom SQL Query

```sql
---- drop tableIF EXISTS #openingbalanceCFD

SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
	 , 'OpeningBalanceCFD' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
,TanganyStatus
,IsDLTUser
-- into #openingbalanceCFD
 FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%CFD%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceCFD'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,IsDLTUser
,TanganyStatus
UNION all

-- drop tableif exists #closingbalanceCFD

SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
	 , 'ClosingBalanceCFD' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue

-- drop tableif exists #calculatedBalanceCFD

SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
	 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_CFD' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
,TanganyStatus
,IsDLTUser

from 
(
		
		SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
			 , 'OpeningBalanceCFD' AS Metric

			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits

,TanganyStatus
,IsDLTUser

		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>

,TanganyStatus
,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all

				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD2
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'InValidZeroCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD3
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'FullCommissionCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD3
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'FullCommissionCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD4
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'SellCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits,
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD4
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'SellCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		
		) a
GROUP BY 
a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	,TanganyStatus
	,IsDLTUser

UNION all

-- drop tableif exists #diffCFD

SELECT 'Gap' AS Category
	 , 'Gap_CFD' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , sum(a.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(a.USDValue  ) as USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	,TanganyStatus
	,IsDLTUser
-- into #diffCFD
FROM 
(
-------------**** calculated close ******* ------------------

SELECT * from (
	SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
	 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_CFD' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	,TanganyStatus
	,IsDLTUser
-- into #calculatedBalanceCFD
from 
(
		
		SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
			 , 'OpeningBalanceCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
			 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		-- into #openingbalanceCFD
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>
		AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%CFD%'
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			,TanganyStatus
			,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'BuyCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'BuyCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD1
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'ValidZeroCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD1
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'ValidZeroCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD2
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category 
			 , 'InValidZeroCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD2
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'InValidZeroCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD3
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'FullCommissionCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD3
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'FullCommissionCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop tableif exists #txCFD4
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'SellCFD' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits,
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyCFD','ValidZeroCFD','InValidZeroCFD', 'FullCommissionCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellCFD') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txCFD4
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'SellCFD'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		) a
GROUP BY 
a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser) obc
UNION ALL 
	SELECT obc.Category
			   , obc.Metric
			   , obc.PositionType
			   , obc.Name
			   , obc.PositionTiming
			   , -1 * obc.TotalUnits AS TotalUnits
			   , -1 * obc.USDValue AS USDValue
			   , obc.IsValidCustomer
			   , obc.IsCreditReportValidCB
			   , obc.IsOutlier
			   , obc.OutlierTransition
			   , obc.CFD_Real_Filter 
			   ,TanganyStatus
			   ,IsDLTUser
----- ********  closing balance again ******** -----
			FROM 
	(
			SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
	 , 'ClosingBalanceCFD' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'CFD' AS CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #closingbalanceCFD
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%CFD%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceCFD'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
			) obc
) a
GROUP BY 
	   a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.CFD_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all 


-- drop table if exists #OpeningBalance

SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
	 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #OpeningBalance
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
		bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all

-- drop table if exists #ClosingBalance

SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
	 , 'ClosingBalanceReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #ClosingBalance
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceReal'
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	   bdidb.Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all

-- drop table if exists #txReal

Select 'TX' AS Category
	 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
	 , bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		AS USDValue
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #txReal
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION all

	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		AS USDValue
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
	 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #txReal4
FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
AND (bdidb.Metric = 'StakingBuy')
-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
GROUP BY 
	  bdidb.PositionType
	 , bdidb.Name
	 , bdidb.PositionTiming
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier

	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

	 , - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
		AS TotalUnits
	 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
	 ,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
		AS USDValue
	 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
	 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , bdidb.IsOutlier
	 , bdidb.OutlierTransition

---- ****** calculated balance ********------

-- drop table if exists #calculatedBalance

SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
	 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_Real' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
	 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #calculatedBalance
		from 
		(
			SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
			 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
			 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #OpeningBalance
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>
		AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
		AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
				bdidb.Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all

			 , 'RedeemSell' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				, - SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal8
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemSell')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal9
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'StakingSell' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				,- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('StakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal9
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'StakingSell')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		
		UNION all
		
		-- drop table if exists #txReal10
		
		Select 'TX' AS Category
			 , 'RedeemStakingSell' AS Metric
			 , bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
			,	- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
				AS TotalUnits
			 --, SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal','ValidZeroReal','InValidZeroReal', 'FullCommissionReal', 'StakingBuy','RedeemBuy','RedeemStakingBuy') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				,- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
				AS USDValue
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		-- into #txReal10
		FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
		WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
		AND (bdidb.Metric = 'RedeemStakingSell')
		-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
		GROUP BY 
			  bdidb.PositionType
			 , bdidb.Name
			 , bdidb.PositionTiming
			 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
			 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
			 , bdidb.IsOutlier
			 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
			 ,TanganyStatus
			 ,IsDLTUser
		) a
GROUP BY 
a.Category
	 , a. Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser

UNION ALL 

---- ******* gap ******** ------

-- drop table if exists #diffReal 

SELECT 'Gap' AS Category
	 , 'Gap_Real' AS Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , sum(a.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
	 , sum(a.USDValue  ) as USDValue
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
-- into #diffReal
FROM 
(
SELECT * from (
				SELECT 'Calculated_Close' AS Category
						 , 'Calculated_Closing_Balance_Real' AS Metric
						 , a.PositionType
						 , a.Name
						 , a.PositionTiming
						 , SUM(a.TotalUnits) AS TotalUnits
						 , SUM(a.USDValue) AS USDValue
						 , a.IsValidCustomer
						 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
						 , a.IsOutlier
						 , a.OutlierTransition
						 , a.Real_Real_Filter
						 ,TanganyStatus
						 ,IsDLTUser
					-- into #calculatedBalance
							from 
							(
								SELECT 'OpeningBalance' AS Category
								 , 'OpeningBalanceReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
								 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #OpeningBalance
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]>
							AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
							AND bdidb.Metric = 'OpeningBalanceReal'
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
									bdidb.Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								,TanganyStatus
								,IsDLTUser
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'BuyReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('BuyReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'BuyReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal1
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'ValidZeroReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									AS TotalUnits
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('ValidZeroReal') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal1
							FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
							WHERE bdidb.Date between <[Parameters].[Parameter 3]> and <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
							AND (bdidb.Metric = 'ValidZeroReal')
							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY 
								  bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							
							UNION all
							
							-- drop table if exists #txReal2
							
							Select 'TX' AS Category
								 , 'InValidZeroReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('InValidZeroReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)

									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.USDValue ELSE 0 END)
									AS USDValue
								 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							-- into #txReal2

							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY

								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming

								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser

								 , 'FullCommissionReal' AS Metric
								 , bdidb.PositionType
								 , bdidb.Name
								 , bdidb.PositionTiming
								 , SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('FullCommissionReal') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)
									--- SUM(CASE WHEN Metric IN ('SellReal','RedeemSell','StakingSell','RedeemStakingSell') then bdidb.TotalUnits ELSE 0 END)

								 ,TanganyStatus

							-- into #txReal3

							-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
							GROUP BY

								 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
								 , bdidb.IsOutlier
								 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
								 ,TanganyStatus
								 ,IsDLTUser
							) a
					GROUP BY 
					a.Category
						 , a. Metric
						 , a.PositionType
						 , a.Name
						 , a.PositionTiming
						 , a.IsValidCustomer
						 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
						 , a.IsOutlier
						 , a.OutlierTransition
						 , a.Real_Real_Filter
						 ,TanganyStatus
						 ,IsDLTUser

				) obc
UNION ALL SELECT obc.Category
			   , obc.Metric
			   , obc.PositionType
			   , obc.Name
			   , obc.PositionTiming
			   , -1 * obc.TotalUnits AS TotalUnits
			   , -1 * obc.USDValue AS USDValue
			   , obc.IsValidCustomer
			   , obc.IsCreditReportValidCB
			   , obc.IsOutlier
			   , obc.OutlierTransition
			   , obc.Real_Real_Filter 
			   ,TanganyStatus
			   ,IsDLTUser
							FROM (
								SELECT 'ClosingBalance' AS Category
					 , 'ClosingBalanceReal' AS Metric
					 , bdidb.PositionType
					 , bdidb.Name
					 , bdidb.PositionTiming
					 , sum(bdidb.TotalUnits) as TotalUnits
					 , sum(bdidb.USDValue  ) as USDValue  
					 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
					 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
					 , bdidb.IsOutlier
					 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
					 , 'Real' AS Real_Real_Filter
					 ,TanganyStatus
					 ,IsDLTUser
					-- into #ClosingBalance
					FROM BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_IFRS15_Daily_Balance bdidb
					WHERE bdidb.Date = <[Parameters].[Parameter 4]>
					AND bdidb.Metric LIKE '%Real%'
					AND bdidb.Metric = 'ClosingBalanceReal'
					-- AND bdidb.Name = @name
					GROUP BY 
					   bdidb.Metric
					 , bdidb.PositionType
					 , bdidb.Name
					 , bdidb.PositionTiming
					 , bdidb.IsValidCustomer
					 , bdidb.IsCreditReportValidCB
					 , bdidb.IsOutlier
					 , bdidb.OutlierTransition
					 ,TanganyStatus
					 ,IsDLTUser
				) obc
) a
GROUP BY 
	   a.Category
	 , a.Metric
	 , a.PositionType
	 , a.Name
	 , a.PositionTiming
	 , a.IsValidCustomer
	 , a.IsCreditReportValidCB
	 , a.IsOutlier
	 , a.OutlierTransition
	 , a.Real_Real_Filter
	 ,TanganyStatus
	 ,IsDLTUser
```

## Downstream calculated fields (in embedded datasources)

### Workbook: IFRS15 Crypto Inventory Cycle - Oct 2024 extract Tangany DLT issues

#### Datasource: Daily Breakdown (live query)

- **calc: today**

  ```
  today()
  ```

- **calc: yesterday**

  ```
  today()-1
  ```

#### Datasource: daterange live query

- **calc: default_date**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', TODAY()) - 1
  ```

- **calc: FromDateLive**

  ```
  [FromDateLive]
  ```

- **calc: month_end**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', DATEADD('month', 1, [calc: default_date])) - 1
  ```

- **calc: month_start**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', [calc: default_date])
  ```

- **calc: TodateLive**

  ```
  [ToDateLive]
  ```

- **calc: today**

  ```
  today()
  ```

- **calc:yesterday**

  ```
  today()-1
  ```

#### Datasource: previous month daterange (extract)

- **calc: default_date**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', today()) - 1
  ```

- **calc: month_end**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', DATEADD('month', 1, [calc: default_date])) - 1
  ```

- **calc: month_start**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month', [calc: default_date])
  ```
